- current UDT principles do not select that branch from the retained global alternatives.

The honest frontier is therefore not “one equation short of a complete theory.” UDT still needs an
operational rule that says which complete metric configuration is realized and how, if at all,
matter, dynamics, and dimensional scale arise from it.

## 1. Reading and status rules

This reference follows the labels `DERIVED`, `CHOSE`, `WORKING`, `OPEN`, `CONDITIONAL`, `POSIT`, and
`OBSERVED`. Compound source labels are retained where needed. A result can be exact mathematics and
still be conditional on premises that UDT has not selected.

The controlling source set and SHA-256 values are in `SOURCE_MANIFEST.tsv`. The mechanical claim map
is `CLAIM_DEPENDENCY_LEDGER.tsv`. If this narrative disagrees with a cited source, the source wins.

The macro WR-L lane and particle/carrier lane remain separate. Shared notation is not a derived
coupling. Pre-July-1 material supplies failure provenance only, not affirmative physics.

## 2. Founding and observational inputs

The synchronized July 17 foundation records four central premises:

1. Positional dilation is `FOUNDING`; under H2 it is not demoted by deriving its functional form.
2. Reciprocal-c is `FOUNDING`: `c` and `c^{-1}` are coequal time-length conversion directions.
3. Dual UDT Reciprocity is `FOUNDING`: in the supplied faithful pairing it acts contragrediently.
4. Common-Scale Neutrality is `FOUNDING`: before material scale is selected, a common positive
   local rescaling is calibration.

The finite mirrored cell is binding for the registered static `phi` seal statement. Static `phi`
is odd at the seal and vanishes there while its normal derivative remains free. That statement does
not fix every field, a full coframe lift, topology, boundary action, or charge.

Bootstrap is `WORKING`: realized matter-bearing universes are expected to be complete global
solutions in a narrow total proper-density window. No density value, center, width, root operator,
or selection functional has been derived.

Measured ordinary-regime `c_E` and `G_obs` are observational anchors. They calibrate mass per length;
they do not by themselves select an absolute length or mass.

Exact basis: [cold dispatch](../UDT_NATIVE_ACTION_COLD_ARM_DISPATCH.md) and
[cold packet](../UDT_NATIVE_ACTION_COLD_PACKET.md).

## 3. Reciprocal kinematics

For the dimension-matched comparison pair, the supplied faithful dual formulation is

```text
q = (c dt, dr),
P = diag(u,v),
P^T K P = K.
```

Dual Reciprocity gives `u v = 1`. Positive additive relative depth, consistent composition,
reversal, and a regularity premise then give reciprocal exponentials. Up to a chosen sign and unit,

```text
P(phi) = diag(exp(-phi), exp(+phi)).
```

After choosing a CSN representative, a local Lorentzian quadratic readout, and the relevant slot
identification, the clock/parallel block can be written

```text
g_tt = -exp(-2 phi) c^2,
g_parallel_parallel = exp(+2 phi).
```

The inverse relation and exponential dependence are the derived core. The representative,
Lorentzian readout, full transverse/angular block, sign/unit, observer mechanics, and universal
identification of the parallel slot with `grad(phi)` are not all derived.

The premise reset is important: physical distance is nonnegative, while `phi` is a signed local
field. Earlier negative-distance and overextended `Xmax` observer interpretations are not inherited.
See the [premise reset](../udt_premise_reset_audit_2026-07-19/AUDIT_REPORT.md).

- a complete finite-cell boundary functional;
- a native carrier, source, charge, or mass normalization.

The strongest action statements are conditional classifications:

- `C^2`/Bach is `UNIQUE-CONDITIONAL` inside the explicitly named four-dimensional, exact-local-CSN,
  metric-only, local-covariant, parity-even, curvature-square, unrestricted-variation class.
- EH is `CONDITIONAL` after a physical representative and scale have been selected and the
  metric-only/local/covariant/second-order/Lovelock premises are supplied.
- No bridge from the pre-scale fourth-order class to a post-scale second-order class is derived.

The complete action, variation domain, native source, differentiable boundary action, and normalized
finite-cell mass remain `OPEN`. See the [final action adjudication](../native_action_final_adjudication_2026-07-18/FINAL_ADJUDICATION_REPORT.md)

## 5. The local metric grammar

The metric-led instrument atlas varied ten metric amplitudes and `phi`, then examined every nonempty
combination of the registered Ricci, `phi`-Hessian, gradient-dyad, Ricci-gradient, and Weyl-gradient
instruments. It found a small repeated vocabulary:

- scalar or silent four-space;
- a coupled Lorentzian pair plus two lines (`1+1+2`);
- four separate lines;
- one line plus a three-space (`1+3`);
- a full irreducible four-dimensional weave.

The strongest orchestra observation is that clean Ricci and `phi`-Hessian rank-two splits usually
cross rather than coincide. In all 2,090 clean registered cases their planes shared no line and
together generated the full weave. This is `OBSERVED_BOUNDED`, not an arbitrary-metric theorem or a
physical matter identification.

See the [instrument motif atlas](../udt_instrument_motif_atlas_2026-07-21/AUDIT_REPORT.md).

## 6. Transport, distributions, and what survived across a cell

For a smooth complete family of mutually annihilating metric-self-adjoint projectors `P_a`, define

```text
K = sum_a (nabla_T P_a) P_a.
```

Projector completeness and idempotence give metric skewness of `K` and

```text
[K,P_a] = nabla_T P_a.
```

This is a genuine metric-compatible geometric transport law for projector motifs. It transports
configuration-space subspaces; it is not physical time evolution.

In the frozen path atlas:

- 95,232 identity/family paths were accounted for;
- 93,920 have stable sampled motifs;
- 1,312 contain transitions or uncertainty;
- 83 deterministic populated-stratum anchors were densely integrated;
- 76 pass all numerical gates and seven retain explicit derivative-level margins.

The most orderly distribution family contains 1,536 midpoint-integrable `1+1+2` rows. All remain
sampled-integrable at nine cell nodes. However, they are eight family presentations of only 192
analytic identities with structural mask `M8`: only the `PHI_FIELD` ensemble is active. This is an
orderly `phi` solo, not the full angular orchestra.

See the [motif-to-Hopf audit](../udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md) and
[global assembly atlas](../udt_global_metric_assembly_atlas_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md).

## 7. Global completion and holonomy

The global assembly atlas retains twelve registered classes: physical-boundary intervals, one- and
two-cap completions, determinant-zero and lens alternatives, `S3`, nonprimitive/singular caps,
general `GL(2,Z)` torus bundles, mirror lifts, nonorientable gluing, stratified projector branches,
nonintegrable distributions, and the conditional reciprocal-toric diagonal class.

The atlas distinguishes four different objects:

1. Kato transport of metric-derived projectors;
2. Levi-Civita tangent holonomy of a complete metric;
3. integral lattice monodromy and cap-cycle data;
4. principal-circle characteristic data after a circle action is supplied.

An open analytic path supplies transport, not holonomy. A local plane supplies neither periods nor a
torus. Reciprocity, CSN, finite-cell structure, the static seal, and current bootstrap constrain the
catalogue but do not select one global quotient.

This is the current global stop: `GLOBAL_QUOTIENT_SELECTION_OPEN`.

## 8. The conditional Hopf bridge

The existing particle code is already a genuine three-dimensional Hopfion implementation. It uses
a full `N x N x N` field, a degree-one Hopf seed, all three spatial derivatives, and a Whitehead/Hopf
charge. Static stability is settled only inside the recorded round-`S2`, `L2+L4`, coefficient,
finite-box, fixed-boundary, and discrete-operator premises.

The metric supplies two narrower geometric leads:

- after a conditional four-dimensional Lorentzian conformal readout, every projectivized null cone
  has a celestial `S2` fiber;
- in the separately supplied reciprocal-toric class, metric `phi` instruments recover the angular
  axes, and with periodic circles, opposite primitive caps, a free diagonal or anti-diagonal action,
  orientation, and normalization, the metric-dual quotient is exactly the degree-one historical
  Hopf seed.

Neither result derives the carrier. A fiber is not a section; a section is not a fixed round target;
a quotient is not a deformable matter configuration space; and none of those objects supplies the
`L2+L4` action.

See the [native topology audit](../native_hopfion_topology_audit_2026-07-19/AUDIT_REPORT.md),

## 10. Scale, mass, and density

With only total mass `M_tot`, cell scale `Xmax`, measured `c_E`, measured `G_obs`, and dimensionless
state data, dimensional analysis leaves one independent dimensionless group:

```text
G_obs M_tot / (c_E^2 Xmax).
```

Consequently current relations can select compactness or a dimensionless branch, not an absolute
mass and length. Defining total density as `M_tot/V_tot` adds no independent equation when the same
solution supplies a volume proportional to `Xmax^3`.

The conditional Hopfion makes the same gap visible microscopically:

```text
E(R) = xi A R + kappa B/R,
R_star = sqrt(kappa/xi) sqrt(B/A).
```

Its finite size inherits the coefficient ruler `sqrt(kappa/xi)`. Hopf charge is dimensionless and
does not select that ruler.

A future noncircular density architecture is logically possible:

```text
solve geometry, native matter/mass, boundary, volume and scale together;
rho_solution = M_native[g,fields] / V_proper[g];
require that rho_solution closes the same global bootstrap problem.
```

Here density is an output returned to the same fixed point, not an observed number inserted at the
start. This remains `OPEN_POTENTIAL_FUTURE_SELECTOR` because UDT has no native mass functional,
varied response map, density-center law, or homothety-breaking datum.

See the [scale census](../scale_breaking_closure_census_2026-07-20/AUDIT_REPORT.md),
[matter dimensional inventory](../matter_bootstrap_dimensional_inventory_2026-07-20/AUDIT_REPORT.md),
and [global assembly density ledger](../udt_global_metric_assembly_atlas_2026-07-22/DENSITY_BOOTSTRAP_CIRCULARITY_LEDGER.tsv).

## 11. A working whole-theory interpretation

The following is `WORKING SYNTHESIS`, not a derived theorem:

- `phi` supplies reciprocal depth and, in the mapped ensemble, an orderly foliation tendency.
- Angular, curvature, gradient, and shift sectors normally cross it into a four-dimensional weave.
- Matter-like structure may require a globally persistent organization of that weave rather than a
  separate scalar lump or one privileged local eigendirection.
- Bootstrap may eventually select complete finite-cell organizations rather than locally evolve a
  preselected particle.
- A deformation law, mass, and density would then belong downstream of the selected whole geometry.

This interpretation fits the metric evidence without promoting any missing arrow. It can be wrong:
UDT may require an independent carrier, the full weave may have no matter interpretation, or the
realization rule may enter at a different layer.

## 12. The proposed next metric-led map

The full tangent-space weave motivates—but does not establish—a different representation to inspect.
Twist, flux, holonomy, linking, and boundary charge are naturally expressed through oriented area
elements and differential forms. The metric itself supplies wedge products, the Hodge operation,
Levi-Civita curvature two-forms, and induced transport on bivectors.

The bounded candidate question is:

> When the registered tangent instruments are irreducible, does their complete metric-induced
> action on two-forms preserve any recurring simple bivector, dual pair, closed/co-closed form,
> contact seed, or restricted holonomy structure beyond the universal structure of an arbitrary
> four-dimensional Lorentzian metric?

This is `WORKING`, not evidence that such a structure exists. It must not target a Hopf answer. A
valid atlas must retain every induced motif, explicitly separate real/complex Hodge structure,
test bivector simplicity and closure, transport stable branches, and classify universal controls.
Rediscovering only the universal Hodge split is a negative for UDT-specific emergence.

An independent but related global question is whether full reciprocal coframe transport around a
selected finite-cell seam could impose a monodromy consistency condition. That question cannot be
posed physically until the seam/loop itself is selected or all retained completions are tested in
parallel.

## 13. Why a realization principle remains central

The current premises define a class of allowed kinematics and global constraints. They do not yet
define a complete mathematical solution concept. Bootstrap says that the realized universe closes
self-consistently, but does not specify whether closure is:

- a fixed point of a whole-solution map;
- stationarity of a functional;
- a two-ended boundary eigenproblem;
- reciprocal transport/holonomy closure;
- or another operation.

Formalizing one of those without a source derivation would invent a premise. The next conceptual
audit should therefore ask what operational content is already implicit in the registered word
“bootstrap,” and where an additional datum is genuinely unavoidable.

# Append-only correction and qualification layer

Date: 2026-07-22  
Applies to frozen reference commit: `1a41c4b`  
Review status: four independent `PASS-WITH-CAVEATS` returns  
Authority: reviewer-informed navigation qualification; cited source evidence still controls.

Nothing in `REFERENCE_FREEZE_MANIFEST.tsv` is rewritten. The statuses in the frozen claim and join
ledgers remain unchanged. This layer narrows wording, makes hidden mathematical distinctions
explicit, and reorders the candidate next questions.

## Q01 — projector transport is universal mathematics instantiated by UDT data

`C032` remains `DERIVED_REGISTERED_GEOMETRIC_IDENTITY`. The Kato/projector connection theorem is a
universal pseudo-Riemannian identity for any smooth complete fixed-rank family of mutually
annihilating metric-self-adjoint projectors. The UDT-specific observation is that the registered
metric/`phi` instruments instantiate particular projector families and sampled paths. The theorem
alone cannot bridge `J02`; a UDT-specific bridge would require a non-universal invariant persisting
on a complete admissible closed branch.

## Q02 — the twelve global rows overlap

`C040` remains `OBSERVED_BOUNDED_TAXONOMY`, but “twelve completion classes” is shorthand for a
twelve-row registered completion/behavior taxonomy. It is not a partition into twelve mutually
exclusive topological families. `FC12` overlaps boundary and cap rows; `FC10` and `FC11` classify
distribution behavior rather than topology. `C041` remains `OPEN_NOT_SELECTED`.

## Q03 — the conditional Hopf sign is not selected

`C050` remains `EXACT_CONDITIONAL`. With the full integral toric basis, `2 pi` periods, reciprocal
range, smooth opposing primitive caps, effective free diagonal or anti-diagonal action,
orientation, and normalization supplied, the conditional bundle has `|c1|=1`. Calling it
degree `+1` requires an orientation/chirality convention; the anti-diagonal branch carries the
opposite sign under the registered convention. This is seed-level bundle geometry, not carrier
emergence.

## Q04 — the broad bivector proposal must be typed and nonduplicative

`C090` stays `WORKING`; `J03` stays `WORKING_NEXT_QUESTION`. A “complete bivector atlas” is too
broad unless it distinguishes three inequivalent constructions:

1. the derivation lift of tangent endomorphisms to `Lambda^2`;
2. exterior-power transport `Lambda^2 U`;
3. the curvature operator `R: Lambda^2 -> Lambda^2`.

Wedge product belongs to exterior algebra, not to the metric. A global ordinary Hodge star also
requires orientation; nonorientable retained completions require local or orientation-line-valued
formulations. The universal Lorentzian Hodge complex structure, Pluecker simplicity cone, induced
pairing, `nabla star=0`, curvature symmetries, and Bianchi identities earn no UDT-specific credit.

The earlier joint invariant-subspace atlas already found zero isolated real simple Riemann or Weyl
eigenbivector planes in all 6,144 registered two-jets. Any new work must hash-link and reuse that
bounded negative. The smallest nonduplicative geometry step is therefore a typed representation
audit, followed only by residual tests requiring the jets, paths, or loops actually available.

## Q05 — the global audit must test cocycles and seams before holonomy claims

`J04` remains `OPEN`. Its bounded test must explicitly cover transition maps, double/triple-overlap
cocycles, seal involution, coframe and metric value/first-jet matching, cap extension, connection
gluing, and only then holonomy on supplied closed loops. Characteristic classes may be evaluated
only when their required orientation, spin, or principal-bundle data are actually supplied.
Distinct invariant values classify branches; they do not rank them without an additional UDT
premise.

## Q06 — realization is prior to the action fork

`J12` remains `OPEN`, but pre-scale versus post-scale variation is the smallest discriminator only
inside a variational realization branch. The mathematically prior question is whether realization
is variational at all. Registered Reciprocity, CSN, finite-cell/seal data, and bootstrap constrain
admissibility but currently supply no operator, relation, functional, fixed-point map, boundary
problem, codomain, or solution/uniqueness criterion.

The minimum missing datum can be stated neutrally as a carrier-free realization relation such as
`R[g]=0` or `g=B[g]`, together with domain, CSN/gauge equivalence, boundary domain, codomain, and
acceptance criterion. Writing such a relation does not derive it. The immediate audit is whether
any part of that datum is already entailed by registered post-firewall UDT evidence.

## Q07 — simultaneous density is potentially, not automatically, noncircular

`C073` remains `OPEN_POTENTIAL_FUTURE_SELECTOR`; `J09` remains `OPEN`. Simultaneity alone does not establish noncircularity. A calculation would require a derived response operator returning a
complete global solution, a native differentiable mass functional and normalized generator, and
an independently derived homothety-breaking datum or process. Without those, `rho=M/V` is only a
definition on a chosen solution and cannot select absolute scale. `J08`, with prerequisites `J04`
and `J06`–`J07`, remains the immediate upstream mass gate.

## Corrected priority

1. Source-only realization-operator audit of the registered word “bootstrap.”
2. Typed induced-representation audit, reusing the existing curvature-eigenbivector negative and
   treating universal Lorentzian structure as a zero-credit control.
3. Neutral cocycle/seam/first-jet/connection-gluing audit across every row of the overlapping global
   taxonomy.
4. Only after a realization branch exists: revisit the pre-scale/post-scale action fork.
5. Only after native source and normalized boundary generator: mass, scale, and simultaneous
   density closure.

This priority is a recommendation, not authorization to launch the next audit.

# Ponder readout — what the whole map now says

Date: 2026-07-22  
Grade: `EXTERNALLY_AUDITED_SYNTHESIS_WITH_CAVEATS`  
This is a lay interpretation and priority recommendation, not canon or a new derivation.

## What we learned

The metric program has not been empty drilling. It has established three useful layers:

1. The reciprocal beginning is real and mathematically coherent within its exact premises.
2. When all metric sectors interact, they normally make a genuine four-dimensional weave rather
   than secretly preserving one preferred clock/ruler or angular plane.
3. Several orderly local and global motifs exist, including a conditional Hopf-compatible branch,
   but the present UDT rules do not choose one complete branch as the universe.

The four cold reviewers agreed that this is an honest picture. Their caveats reveal that our first
proposed follow-up—“map all bivectors”—was still too broad. Much of what one sees on two-forms is
automatic for any four-dimensional Lorentzian metric, and an earlier audit has already found no
isolated real simple curvature-eigenbivector plane in the registered 6,144 two-jets. Repeating that
search under a broader name would create activity, not progress.

## The likely hidden-in-plain-sight gap

UDT currently describes an allowed orchestra of complete metrics, but it does not yet define what
it means for one score to be the performance that actually occurs.

“Bootstrap” presently says the realized universe must be globally self-consistent. It does not yet
say what operation performs that self-consistency test. Is it a fixed point, a boundary relation,
an eigenproblem, stationarity of an action, a transport closure, or something else? Choosing one by
mathematical taste would invent a rule. But checking the registered UDT statements to see whether
one is already implicit is a small, decisive audit.

In lay terms: we have mapped many shapes the metric can make. We still lack the native sentence
that says, “this is how nature chooses which complete shape exists.” That may be the elegant missing
piece—or the audit may show plainly that one additional premise is unavoidable.

## Recommended order

### 1. Realization-operator audit — first

Without solving anything, take every registered statement about Reciprocity, CSN, the finite cell,
the seal, and bootstrap. Test whether it supplies each part of a well-posed selection relation:
input class, equivalence/gauge, operation, boundary domain, output, and acceptance or uniqueness
criterion. Compare fixed-point, boundary/eigenvalue, variational, holonomy, and “no operator
supplied” formulations neutrally.

Maximum honest result: either a specific component is already `DERIVED`, or bootstrap remains
on-shell admissibility and the realization operator stays `OPEN`.

### 2. Typed metric representation audit — second

If metric mapping continues, separate three different questions that had been bundled together:
how tangent operators act on area elements, how those area elements are transported, and how
curvature acts on them. Reuse the prior negative result, declare orientation explicitly, and give
no scientific credit for universal Hodge or exterior-algebra identities.

Maximum honest result: a bounded non-universal recurring metric motif—or a clean negative.

### 3. Global cocycle and seam audit — third

For every retained taxonomy row, test whether its local pieces can actually be glued into a smooth
complete geometry: transition consistency, seal and first-derivative matching, cap extension,
connection gluing, and holonomy only where a real closed loop is supplied. This can eliminate
inconsistent candidates but cannot favor a pretty topology merely because it resembles matter.

### 4. Action, matter, and scale remain downstream

The `C^2` versus EH fork becomes decisive only if the realization rule is variational. Density is
not automatically noncircular just because it is solved simultaneously. Native mass, a normalized
boundary generator, a complete response operator, and genuine scale breaking are still missing.
No current eigenvalue, topology, or normalized geometric quantity fixes absolute scale.

## Bottom line

The promising possibility is not that one more large scan will suddenly output the full theory. It
is that the map has isolated a concise conceptual seam: **admissibility is not yet realization**.
That seam is now more important than GPU exploration, time-live soliton work, or another untargeted
solution-space expansion.

No follow-on audit is launched by this readout. Charles must authorize the next bounded scientific
step.

# Lay report — what the global assembly map found

We now know how the local geometric “instruments” can be carried continuously from place to place.
The transport preserves both the geometric directions and the metric used to measure them. This is
real mathematical progress: the motifs are no longer merely unrelated snapshots.

One orderly family also survived a stronger test. Every candidate that looked like two clean
complementary surfaces at the midpoint still looked that way at all nine sampled positions.

But its provenance matters. All those candidates came from the test in which only `phi` was playing.
The metric’s base, angular, and shift sections were silent. The 1,536 rows are eight mathematical
descriptions of 192 underlying `phi`-only configurations. So we found a coherent `phi` foliation,
not yet the full orchestra organizing itself into angular circles.

We then catalogued the ways a finite geometry could close globally. It can retain physical
boundaries, close one circle, close the same circle at both ends, close opposite circles, form lens
spaces, glue into periodic torus bundles, use different mirror actions, become nonorientable, retain
an anholonomic twisting plane, or pass through points where the fine projector pattern changes.
The familiar `S3`/Hopf completion is one exact conditional member of that much larger territory.

The current UDT rules constrain this atlas but do not choose one member. Reciprocity controls the
opposing dilation pattern. CSN removes common scale. The finite-cell principle removes spatial
infinity. The seal constrains `phi` in its static setting. Bootstrap asks a complete universe to be
self-consistent. None currently says which circles exist, how they close, which quotient to take, or
what action governs a deformable quotient.

That is why we did not proceed to a time-dependent matter solve. Doing so would require us to choose
the missing global structure and dynamics ourselves.

The density/bootstrap idea has a sensible future form. Density should not be guessed first. A
complete UDT solution would produce its own mass and proper volume; their ratio would then feed back
into the same global consistency condition. That could resolve the chicken-and-egg problem as a
simultaneous fixed point. At present we can describe the possible volumes and boundaries, but UDT's
native mass numerator is still missing.

The honest picture is therefore:

- continuous metric-motif transport: derived and numerically mapped, with seven margins retained;
- coherent cell-wide sampled foliation: observed, but it is `phi`-only;
- global completion and holonomy territory: catalogued for the registered families;
- one globally selected quotient: not found;
- carrier/action emergence and physical time evolution: not yet activated;
- density as a future simultaneous bootstrap output: promising architecture, still open.

The key clue is now sharper. The obstacle is not simply carrying local structure across the cell.
The obstacle is getting the full metric orchestra—not the `phi` solo—to organize into a globally
closed quotient under a law UDT itself supplies.

# UDT Global Metric-Assembly Atlas

Date: 2026-07-22

Status: `VERIFIED_WITH_REGISTERED_NUMERIC_MARGINS__FRESH_CORRECTION_REVIEW_PASS`

Maximum conclusion:

`BOUNDED_REGISTERED_GLOBAL_METRIC_ASSEMBLY_ATLAS_CHARACTERIZED__GLOBAL_QUOTIENT_SELECTION_OPEN`

## Result first

The atlas closes the first four requested mapping stages inside its preregistered registry, audits
the fifth selector stage, and stops at the activation gates for Stages 6 and 7.

The most important positive result is a metric-compatible continuous transport law for any smooth
complete projector motif. For mutually annihilating metric-self-adjoint projectors `P_a`, define

```text
K = sum_a (nabla_T P_a) P_a,
nabla_T U = K U.
```

Differentiating projector completeness and idempotence gives

```text
K is metric-skew,
[K,P_a] = nabla_T P_a.
```

Therefore `U` preserves the endpoint metric and intertwines the projector subspaces. This is a
native geometric connection for the motif bundles. It is not physical time evolution.

Across all 83 populated stable `(motif,instrument-family)` strata, deterministic dense anchors were
integrated at 33, 65, and 129 nodes. Seventy-six pass all preregistered transport gates. Seven retain
strict derivative-level numerical margins; their endpoint intertwining, metric-isometry, and RK4
refinement residuals remain small, but they are not promoted. Exact symbolic Lorentzian and
reciprocal-toric controls pass, and a separate `DOP853` implementation independently reproduces one
`FOUR_LINES`, one `LINE_PLUS_THREE`, and one `TWO_PLUS_TWO_LINES` transport anchor.

The finite-cell-path follow-up also found a coherent subfamily. Every one of the 1,536 frozen
midpoint-integrable `1+1+2` identity/family rows remains locally integrable on both complementary
rank-two sides at all nine sampled path nodes. This is not a midpoint accident.

Its provenance sharply limits the interpretation: all 1,536 rows come from structural mask `M8`,
where only `PHI_FIELD` is active. They are eight instrument-family presentations of 192 analytic
identities. Thus the coherent integrable branch is the orderly `phi`-field/Hessian solo already
suspected to form nested surfaces. It is not a full metric-angular orchestra, not two commuting
periodic generators, and not a metric-derived torus or carrier.

The global taxonomy retains 12 parametric completion families, including physical boundaries,
one-cap boundaries, determinant-zero same-cycle caps, determinant-one `S3`, all determinant-`p>1`
lens families, nonprimitive/singular caps, general `GL(2,Z)` torus bundles, mirror lifts,
nonorientable gluing, projector strata, nonintegrable distributions, and the conditional globally
diagonal reciprocal-toric class. No family is removed for failing to resemble matter or the desired
universe.

Registered Reciprocity, Common-Scale Neutrality, finite-cell/seal data, bootstrap, and the current
scale/matter inventory do not select one quotient class. Accordingly:

- Stage 6: `NOT_ACTIVATED__GLOBAL_QUOTIENT_NOT_SELECTED`;
- Stage 7: `NOT_ACTIVATED__NATIVE_DYNAMICS_UNDEFINED`;
- CPU time-live evolution runs: `0`;
- GPU runs: `0`.

## Stage 1 — continuous projector transport

The frozen atlas contains 95,232 identity/family paths:

| stable motif | paths |
|---|---:|
| full irreducible four-dimensional weave | 70,812 |
| scalar/silent | 11,328 |
| `1+1+2` | 7,845 |
| `1+3` | 2,880 |
| four lines | 1,055 |

There are 93,920 stable sampled paths and 1,312 transition or uncertain paths. All appear exactly
once in `PATH_ASSEMBLY_CENSUS.tsv.gz`. Transition paths receive no invented fine bundle.

The connection theorem follows directly from the complete projector algebra. With
`sum_a P_a=I`, `P_a P_b=delta_ab P_a`, and metric compatibility:

```text
K^dagger = sum_a P_a nabla_T P_a = -K,
[K,P_a] = nabla_T P_a.
```

The numerical equation in coordinates is

```text
dU/ds = (K-Gamma_T) U.
```

The dense-anchor census is:

| status | anchors |
|---|---:|
| `DENSE_TRANSPORT_PASS` | 76 |
| `DENSE_TRANSPORT_NUMERIC_MARGIN_RETAINED` | 7 |

The seven margins are listed in `NUMERIC_MARGIN_LEDGER.tsv`. They arise in finite-difference checks
of the exact metric-skew/commutator identities. The largest endpoint metric-isometry residual among
them is about `2.26e-9`, and the largest 65-to-129-node transport refinement is about `1.39e-7`.
The largest derivative identity residual is about `2.85e-6`, above the fixed `2e-7` gate. The exact
theorem remains valid; those numerical rows remain unresolved at the registered threshold.

Scalar and full-irreducible motifs transport the whole tangent space but supply no distinguished
proper subbundle. An open path supplies transport, not holonomy.

## Stage 2 — following the locally integrable candidates

The frozen midpoint atlas contains:

- 8,205 `1+1+2` identity/family rows;
- 6,669 with nonintegrable Lorentz/two-line complementary planes at the midpoint;
- 1,536 with both sides integrable there.

All 1,536 candidate rows were followed at `t=j/8`, `j=0..8`, retaining the original two stencil
steps and thresholds. The result is exactly 13,824 node rows, all
`BOTH_SIDES_SAMPLED_INTEGRABLE`.

The complete provenance is:

```text
structural mask: M8 = PHI_FIELD only
unique analytic identities: 192
instrument-family presentations per identity: 8
identity/family rows: 1,536
```

The eight families all contain `H`; any listed `R`, `RG`, or `WG` operator is zero in this
structural mask. This is why the rows must not be interpreted as 1,536 independent geometric
mechanisms. The result strengthens the `phi`-foliation observation and simultaneously weakens its
claim to be the missing angular/Hopf assembly.

The generic full orchestra remains dominated by the irreducible four-dimensional weave. The exact
reciprocal-toric axis/Hopf witness is consequently still a special conditional commuting stratum,
not a branch selected or even reproduced by the `PHI_FIELD`-only integrable census.

## Stage 3 — global completion catalogue

`COMPLETION_CLASS_REGISTRY.tsv` records 12 parametric families. Infinite cap and monodromy families
are represented by exact rules plus bounded arithmetic witnesses.

The cap witness census uses every canonical primitive vector with coefficients bounded by three,
giving 256 ordered pairs:

| class | bounded witnesses |
|---|---:|
| dependent/same-cycle `p=0` | 16 |
| determinant-one `S3` | 58 |
| lens `p>1` | 182 |

These counts are arithmetic controls, not frequencies and not an exhaustion of the infinite cap
family. The exact general rule remains `p=|det(v_-,v_+)|`.

Eight explicit `GL(2,Z)` controls cover identity, finite elliptic, parabolic, hyperbolic, and
orientation-reversing mapping-torus classes. The parametric family is not reduced to those eight
witnesses. Their corrected class census is three finite elliptic witnesses (including the exact
order-two element `-I`), one nontrivial parabolic witness, one identity, one hyperbolic witness, and
two orientation-reversing witnesses.

Every one of seven motif/transition/control classes is crossed with every completion family in the
84-row `MOTIF_COMPLETION_ATLAS.tsv`. A cross-row records compatibility requirements; it is not an
assertion that the local analytic polynomial already supplies a complete global metric witness.

## Stage 4 — bundle and holonomy data

The atlas keeps four objects separate:

1. Kato transport of metric-derived projector bundles;
2. Levi-Civita tangent holonomy of a complete metric;
3. integral torus-lattice monodromy and cap-cycle data; and
4. principal-circle characteristic data after a free circle action is supplied.

The local analytic paths provide object 1. They do not close into loops and therefore do not supply
holonomy. The completion registry supplies parametric data for object 3. Object 2 remains
profile-dependent until a complete metric is supplied. Object 4 exists only in the conditional
reciprocal-toric control after periods, action, caps, orientation, and normalization are disclosed.

In that control, the depth-path coordinate projectors are covariantly constant, so their Kato
generator is zero. The metric-dual principal connection still has the separate normalized fraction

```text
f(phi)=1/(1+exp(4 phi)),
Q_finite=f(phi_minus)-f(phi_plus).
```

Common angular scale cancels, but finite endpoints remain boundary-dependent. Unit class remains
conditional on the full global premises.

## Stage 5 — registered UDT selector audit

The 84-row selector matrix applies seven exact selector/status axes to all 12 completion families.

- Reciprocity constrains reciprocal ratios and transition parity. It does not supply a cover,
  periods, cap vectors, orientation, or a circle action.
- CSN removes positive common scale from normalized pre-material structure. It does not select a
  topology; its cancellation from the toric connection is compatibility, not selection.
- The finite-cell canon removes spatial infinity and supplies a physical mirrored-cell setting. It
  does not choose retained boundary versus cap, cap cycles, or a complete seal lift.
- The static seal statement constrains `phi`, while several complete coframe/angular lifts survive.
- Current bootstrap is on-shell admissibility. It has no off-shell functional that ranks the atlas
  branches.
- Current scale/matter evidence supplies no native carrier, mass, source, normalized boundary
  charge, or action coefficient that could close the selection loop.
- Density cannot be a native selector while its mass numerator is undefined.

Multiple current-compatible or conditional branches therefore remain. `S3` and the free Hopf
action remain unique only inside their previously supplied toric eigencap premises.

## Density/bootstrap chicken-and-egg audit

The density issue has a type-correct possible resolution, but not yet an equation.

The desired noncircular closure would solve the complete geometry, native matter fields, physical
scale, boundary data, and bootstrap simultaneously, then define

```text
rho_solution = M_native[g,fields] / V_proper[g]
```

from that same solution. Requiring the resulting density to reproduce the branch that generated it
could be a genuine fixed-point or eigenvalue condition. Density would be an output fed back in a
simultaneous solve, not an observed number inserted at the start.

The assembly atlas can supply branch-dependent candidate volume and boundary objects. It supplies no
native mass functional. Current compactness relations also remain rank one: writing density as
`M/V` does not create an independent scale equation when `V` scales as `X_max^3`.

Accordingly the simultaneous density/bootstrap route is a `POTENTIAL_FUTURE_SELECTOR`, while its
native mass, varied closure, response map, and independent scale breaking remain `OPEN`.

## Stages 6 and 7

The preregistered gate for Stage 6 requires one selected quotient together with its distribution,
gluing/periodicity, action, orientation status, and boundary completion. That gate fails because no
quotient is selected. No configuration space or metric-induced reduced action was invented.

Stage 7 additionally requires a native nonlinear evolution law, constraints, boundary flux, and raw
residual. Those objects are absent. No relaxation trajectory was relabeled as time, no CPU
time-evolution solve was run, and GPU work was not launched.

## How we work (binding method — Charles, 2026-06-14)

The bottleneck has been the METHOD, not the physics. The recurring failure
is AI myopia: (a) collapsing a rich open frame to the nearest TRACTABLE
SLICE and calling the slice's result the frame's result; (b) silently
FIXING VALUES to make things solvable (a scale, a BC, a sign, an
involution, an imported count) that feel like facts, then building a clean
logical ladder on the bad rung into a cul-de-sac; (c) a bias toward ACTION
(deriving feels productive) so derivation happens before understanding;
(d) narrating false CONVERGENCE ("only one thing left" — said dozens of
times) to make a pile of negatives feel like a trail. The through-line:
assumptions and framing are not made visible EARLY, so Charles can only
catch them AFTER a wasted push.

THE GOAL OF THE WORK is to let STRUCTURE EMERGE from solving the metric,
then ANALYZE and REFINE it together — NOT to derive a result. Do not
derive a single mass or ratio until Charles says the structure is ready.
Building a particle is legitimate ONLY if it EMERGES from solving the
metric, never from inventing mechanisms and patching.

INVERT THE DEFAULT from "derive/launch" to "make-visible-and-ponder."
Four modes, in order; OBSERVE/PONDER are primary, DERIVE is gated:
1. MAP (first, no compute). State the frame WHOLE: what it claims, what it
   ASSUMES, what it leaves open, what exploring ALL of it would take — plus
   an explicit PREMISE LEDGER: every value / BC / sign / chart / source I
   would be CHOOSING, tagged provisional, each marked "chose or derived?".
   Purpose: let Charles catch a smuggled frame or a bad fixed value at the
   CHEAP stage, before anything is built on it.
2. OBSERVE (primary). Agents solve the metric in a regime and report WHAT
   IS THERE — not "show X." Let structure emerge; report it with premises
   attached. No verdict-hunting.
3. PONDER (with Charles). Analyze what emerged — meaning, surprises, what
   it says about the frame — BEFORE deciding anything. Deliverable =
   understanding. More zooming out and pondering, less deriving.
4. DERIVE (gated, last). Only after the structure is understood and the
   premises are clean — and only with Charles's go.

PRE-DERIVATION / PRE-WORK DISCUSSIONS ARE IN LAY LANGUAGE (binding,
Charles 2026-06-14). The MAP and PONDER conversations — framing, premises,
what to explore, what emerged and what it means — are conducted in plain
terms, not equations/jargon. (Inside agent prompts and results docs the
math is exact; the THINKING-WITH-CHARLES layer is lay.)

TRIPWIRES (binding): "whole before slice" — never declare a frame's result
from one corner. "Chose or derived?" — every fixed value gets the tag, out
loud, before use. "Observing or targeting?" — asked before every agent
launch; if targeting a desired answer, STOP and ponder. Refusal/elimination
RUN -> mandatory zoom-out and REFRAME, never "one more thing." Count the
run; a string of negatives indicts the QUESTION/method, not "the next
place to drill." "Mismatch -> SOLVER, not MECHANISM" — see below.

MISMATCH -> SOLVER, NOT MECHANISM (binding, Charles 2026-06-19). When a result
is far from observation, the FIRST hunt is the SOLVER and our application of
it — NEVER a mechanism. In order: (1) what did we leave OUT of the solver (a
term/coupling/sector/boundary); (2) is it a NUMERIC problem (convergence,
box-control, conditioning, a bug, grid); (3) did we FREEZE or forget to turn
on a degree of freedom; (4) have we explored the solution space with
EVERYTHING ON, or only a corner — plus the many WAYS to examine the same solve
(bases, grids, seeds, continuation, gauge tests, independent re-derivation).
Reaching for a MECHANISM to close a gap is FORBIDDEN until the solver is
demonstrably complete and the solution space genuinely explored. A mismatch
indicts the solver's COMPLETENESS first, the metric last, and a mechanism
never (that is the import reflex). This is Principle 1 applied to our own
numerics. (Historical instrument = `archive/SOLVER_COMPLETENESS_MAP.md`; forward frame =
`archive/POST_POSTULATE_PROGRAM.md` — both ARCHIVED/subsumed now the static solver is code-complete;
the live status is LIVE.md + `pytest tests/`.)
SCAR it heads off: the year-long catalog/mechanism hunt that read a graveyard
of contaminated/classical-solver negatives as a verdict on the metric;
microphysics was UNENTERED, not walled.

SOLUTION-SPACE, NOT IMPOSITION (binding, Charles 2026-06-25). The simple goal:
perform PURE MATH and explore the metric's solution space for WHAT EMERGES,
which LATER we consider as physics. The recurring drift (multiple times in ~2
weeks): we slide from EXPLORING the solution space to IMPOSING the physics we
expect. The purity gate catches IMPORTS; this catches IMPOSITIONS. Before any
solve/result: (a) tag every BC / matter-sector / coupling / acceptance criterion
as free-and-explored, pinned-by-THEORY (cite it), or pinned-by-HABIT (= drift
flag — free or justify); (b) ask "does this diagnostic CHARACTERIZE the solution
or FILTER it (demand a shape / smoothness / a lump / the expected answer)?" — a
filter throws solutions away and is an imposition; (c) "observing or TARGETING?"
checked against the SM-template list (lump/mass/particle/spectrum). GOVERNING
LIMIT — any gate/guard/lint we build to enforce this may check only PROVENANCE
(numeric-vs-smuggled import; derived-vs-pinned value) and HONESTY (is the pin
tagged/surfaced) — NEVER MERIT (is the solution the right shape). A check that
judges merit becomes a blocker that imposes, and that judgment accumulates into
the very drift we fight; merit is judged LATER, with Charles. This limit is
enforced BY HAND (verifier), deliberately not by a machine meta-test (a label is
satisfiable by a drifting author; a binding principle is not). Skill =
`solution-space-not-imposition`; gate = `tests/test_solution_space_gate.py`
(numeric-only imports + premise-ledger tags, both physics-blind). [[solution-space-not-imposition]]

DIVISION OF LABOR (honest): the driver genuinely cannot always see its own
smuggled assumptions — Charles holding the frame is irreplaceable, the
verifier catches errors/assembly. The method does not remove this; it moves
the catching-surface EARLIER by front-loading the frame-map + premise
ledger so Charles steers at the assumption stage, not after the build.

## Discipline skills (full-form protocols — P3, 2026-06-23)

The binding disciplines above are kept INLINE here as short tripwires (always in context). Their
EXPANDED, self-contained full-form lives as auto-loading skills in `.claude/skills/` — invoke the
relevant one at the relevant moment (the inline tripwire is the trigger, the skill is the protocol):
- **`solver-first`** — the mismatch -> SOLVER-not-MECHANISM four-question protocol (run on any
  result far from observation, BEFORE reaching for a mechanism).
- **`verifier-before-record`** — what a clean blind adversarial pass requires (run before committing
  ANY result; fresh zero-context, re-run, hunt false passes, redo the catch-proof, verdict).
- **`no-shortcuts`** — the anti-import/anti-freeze checklist + `python3 -m pytest tests/` (the P1+P2
  purity harness; run when building/editing solver code or before banking a result).
- **`completeness-map`** — the ten completeness criteria + standing questions (run every push;
  every result is ONE tile). (Old instrument `archive/SOLVER_COMPLETENESS_MAP.md` — archived; live
  status = LIVE.md + `pytest tests/`.)
- **`solution-space-not-imposition`** — the 4-point anti-imposition audit (ansatz/BC ledger;
  characterize-not-filter; observe-not-target; solution-space completeness) + the PROVENANCE/
  HONESTY-never-MERIT limit on any gate we build (run before any solve/result). Gate =
  `tests/test_solution_space_gate.py`.

(Skills are the expandable text; the inline tripwires remain binding and always-loaded — the skills
do NOT replace them, they unfold them on demand.)

## DRIVER TRIGGERS (binding, always-loaded — fire WITHOUT being challenged)

The cognitive corral above is recall-class: this session it fired only when Charles challenged, not on
its own (the driver drifted to a "cured" headline; the verifier caught it). These triggers fix that:
each binds to an OBSERVABLE SELF-OUTPUT TOKEN the driver is about to write — you cannot emit the token
without owing the procedure. They force a PAUSE + HONESTY/PROVENANCE; they NEVER judge MERIT (is the
answer the right shape / a lump / the expected mass). (Spec: COGNITIVE_CORRAL_TRIGGERS_SETUP.md.)

**LEAVES ROOM FOR THE WORK — the allowed lane (binding; no trigger may fire to block these).** These
triggers police the SMUGGLE OF PHYSICS, never the BORROWING OF METHOD. CATEGORY-A (conditioning /
numerical technique / *how* we solve) is ALWAYS GREEN and only needs a soundness/convergence check:
borrowing JFNK/Newton-Krylov, continuation/homotopy, spectral/collocation, preconditioners, junction-
condition/DtN/Calderón & geon formalism, machine-precision Taylor replacement — and USING GR AS A
REFERENCE/LIMIT (flat/Schwarzschild/de Sitter anchors, contrasting to see where UDT departs). A technique
changes HOW we solve the UDT equations, not the physics: it is NOT a "mechanism/term/coupling" (does not
trip #2) and need NOT be "derived from the metric" (does not trip #5); only two duties — apply it to the
UDT equations (don't silently swap in GR's), and soundness-check it. CATEGORY-B (a change to the PHYSICS
— a mechanism, coupling, equation-form, source, or a structure-holding BC) is gated. Default for a real
technique or a GR-as-reference comparison is GREEN; progress is the point. *(This clause is non-droppable
and MUST travel verbatim with any cross-check payload / local-LLM export — a "forbid"-only half over-blocks.)*

Each: **TRIGGER** (the tokens/moment) → **STOP-AND-DO**.
1. **Purist-logic / anti-tractable-slice.** TRIGGER: before recommending an approach, or writing
   *easiest / simplest / just / cleaner / for now / tractable*. STOP-AND-DO: name the PUREST/least-imposed
   option AND the easy one, with the objective cost of each; if the pure option is blocked by a flaw
   (grid limit, frozen DOF, an import), the action is FIX THE FLAW — name it, refuse the shortcut (legal
   only as an explicitly-ledgered temporary stand-in). THEN recommend. [[apply-purist-logic-proactively]]
2. **Solver-first, not mechanism.** TRIGGER: before proposing a new mechanism/coupling/term/BC to explain
   a gap, or writing *maybe if we add / a mechanism / what if the metric also*. STOP-AND-DO: run the four
   solver questions — (1) what did we leave OUT? (2) is it NUMERIC (convergence/conditioning/grid/bug)?
   (3) did we FREEZE a DOF? (4) explored the whole space with everything ON? Mechanism FORBIDDEN until the
   solver is demonstrably complete; mismatch indicts solver first, metric last, mechanism never. [[solver-first-not-mechanism]]
3. **Whole before slice.** TRIGGER: before reporting a result, or writing *the metric does / this shows /
   scale-free / no localization / featureless / continuum*. STOP-AND-DO: name the regime actually solved
   and the FREE choices held fixed (static / diagonal / branch G-or-P / grid / frozen rows); label the
   result SCOPED to that regime. Never state a one-corner result as the frame's verdict. [[sweep-whole-not-fragments]]
4. **Provisional until verified.** TRIGGER: before banking a verdict — committing a result doc, or writing
   *cured / conclusive / confirmed / dead / no-go / proven / it works*. STOP-AND-DO: confirm all four —
   pre-registered? full-space (or bounded slice justified)? blind-verified on the load-bearing premise?
   every forced premise audited? If any is missing, label it PROVISIONAL / a LEAD, not a result. [[session-handoff-pointer]] (verifier-before-record)
5. **Chose or derived.** TRIGGER: before any numeric value / BC / sign / chart enters a solve or a banked
   claim. STOP-AND-DO: tag each FREE / THEORY(cite) / HABIT; a HABIT is a drift flag (free or justify it);
   a result riding a FREE constant is conditioned on it — say so. SCOPE: PHYSICS premises only; conditioning/
   solver params (grid, tol, continuation step, preconditioner) are category-A (soundness, not derivation).
6. **Derive natively, not GR's form.** TRIGGER: before writing *folds away / reduces to the standard case /
   as in GR / vacuum is / the usual Einstein*. STOP-AND-DO: that step is the prime suspect for smuggling GR
   back in — show the term's fate from the positional-dilation operator NATIVELY; do not assume the
   inherited form. (GR as reference is allowed (lane #2); ADOPTING GR's answer as UDT's is the smuggle.) [[derive-natively-not-inherited-form]]

## Session workflow

- **Maximize the use of subagents to preserve main context** (Charles,
  2026-06-10): delegate reconnaissance, implementation, verification, and
  doc-drafting to agents; keep only distilled reports in the main loop.
  Present the process plan before launching long pushes.
- **Use the GPU** (Charles, 2026-06-11): a Tesla V100-PCIE-32GB is
  available via PyTorch (`torch.linalg`, float64, cuda=True; note
  nvidia-smi/NVML is broken — driver mismatch — but torch works fine;
  expect an NVML warning, ignore it). Production eigensolves, scans,
  and flow sweeps should use batched torch float64 (~14 ms per
  1024² symmetric eigensolve batched; 6x single-solve). Keep mpmath/
  sympy on CPU for high-precision anchors and symbolic identities;
  GPU results get CPU spot-checks at a few points per run.
  KNOWN PITFALL (found 2026-06-11): on this V100/cu121 stack, batched
  torch.linalg.solve_triangular with a BROADCAST Cholesky factor
  silently corrupts at large batch (~150+); use explicit inverse +
  batched matmul, and always run per-batch CPU asserts.
- **ANTI-HANG (binding operational rule, 2026-06-20 — SIX+ agents hung this
  way).** The coupled solves are SLOW (jacrev/iteration-bound, minutes to
  ~1700s). ALWAYS run solves BOUNDED: cap the grid (Nr<=16/24), cap Newton/
  Krylov iters, and run a SINGLE clean process at a time — NEVER concurrent
  (GPU contention stalls everything), and NEVER launch-a-solve-and-poll a
  background task (agents hang waiting). Fixed-background eigenproblems are
  cheap (5-22s); the dense-LM (jacrev+lstsq) is the flooring tool; recompute
  on SAVED fields where possible. If a solve would exceed budget, REDUCE and
  report "throughput-limited" — a bounded honest partial beats a hang.
  Stability/landscape tests: NEVER blend a field toward a chosen endpoint and
  call it dynamics (a biased artifact — it cost a wrong headline); use unbiased
  kicks + NEB + a 3-cell persistence test (a 2-cell test throws look-elsewhere
  false positives).

## Repo discipline (use git AS git — Charles 2026-06-24)

- **EDIT files in place; let git history be the audit trail.** Commit per
  logical change with a clear message; roll back via `git revert`/history if a
  change regresses. The point of committing is ROLLBACK capability, not freezing.
  REPEALED (Charles 2026-06-24, "patently absurd... the opposite of using a git
  repository"): the old "committed scripts are immutable / new work = new files /
  research-record markdown append-never-edit" rule. It froze improvement and
  caused SOLVER PROLIFERATION — a stale harnessed path (p1_residual) while the
  live work moved to an un-harnessed file (branchGP). When you improve a solver,
  EDIT it (and update its harness); do not spawn branchGP_v2. Append-only is fine
  for a running LAB-LOG section of a results doc, but correcting/superseding an
  earlier claim by EDITING (with the change visible in git) is now preferred over
  piling addenda. A RECONCILIATION is owed: consolidate the proliferated
  solvers/scripts to ONE canonical solver + its harness, retire the rest.
- **Verifier-before-record**: every result (positive or negative) gets a
  blind adversarial verifier pass, recorded in its results doc with agent
  id and date, before commit.
- **Pre-register before testing**: falsification contracts (frozen model,
  candidate lists, tolerances, look-elsewhere accounting) are committed
  BEFORE the test runs. No retuning after.
- Calibrate, never dramatize. Failures are recorded as failures. Negative
  results are first-class deliverables.
- Null-test discipline: exact rational matches are cheap (small-rational
  coverage ~16-23%, see dimension_ladder_null_audit.md). New value
  identities must pass the TEST-B-style classifier (generalize, solve,
  check N-specificity) before being banked as evidence.
- **Negative results are scoped, never absolute** (Charles, 2026-06-11):
  every banked negative/no-go carries its PREMISE SET (background,
  source treatment, boundary conditions, domain class, truncation,
  method). The living index is NEGATIVES_REGISTRY.md. When any premise
  is later revised or refuted, every negative carrying it is flagged

# Verifier-before-record (binding)

Every result gets a BLIND ADVERSARIAL verifier pass, recorded in its results doc with the
verifier's agent id + date, BEFORE commit. Negative results are first-class — they get the
same pass.

## A clean blind pass requires
- FRESH ZERO-CONTEXT instance (no conversation history). For load-bearing / native-vs-import /
  "must-quantize"-class verdicts, use a fresh instance and/or a different model family (P4) — a
  same-context same-model subagent shares blind spots.
- ADVERSARIAL stance: try to BREAK the claim, not confirm it. Default to skepticism; concede
  only what cannot be refuted.
- INDEPENDENTLY RE-RUN the key computation/tests; report the real numbers vs the claim.
- Hunt FALSE PASSES: tautologies, vacuous asserts, loose tolerances that would pass a broken
  result, circular references, a check that secretly reuses the thing it tests.
- For a test harness: REDO the catch-proof (reintroduce each bug, confirm the matching test
  goes RED). An untested guard is decoration.
- Verdict: VERIFIED / VERIFIED-WITH-CAVEATS / REFUTED, with concrete reasons. Distinguish
  "PROVEN to machine precision" from "CONSISTENCY-checked / REGRESSION-locked."
- Leave the repo EXACTLY as found (restore scratch edits; note UNTRACKED files won't
  `git checkout` back — back them up manually).

## Cross-model escalation (load-bearing calls — P4)
For NATIVE-vs-IMPORT classifications, "must-quantize"-class verdicts, and CANON candidates, ALSO
run a verifier on a DIFFERENT Claude tier (Agent `model=` param, e.g. driver=opus -> sonnet), fresh
zero-context, pointed at the source docs NOT the prior verdict. Log the cross-model agent's
id+model+verdict; a DISAGREEMENT is resolved or escalated to Charles, NEVER dropped — and if it
refines a classification, update the source-of-truth. Protocol = `CROSS_MODEL_VERIFY.md`.

## Aim
Aim verifiers HARDEST at results that CONFIRM the standing hypothesis (hypothesis discipline:
"find what's real, not what confirms priors"). Record caveats; CLOSE or explicitly SCOPE them
before banking. Pre-register falsification contracts before the test runs; no retuning after.

## Whole question

After quotienting the complete registered UDT metric description by allowed
coframe changes and Common-Scale Neutrality, does the metric and its
registered finite-cell data determine any intrinsic:

1. reduction of the tangent, coframe, conformal-frame, or associated bundle;
2. section or multisection of the conditional celestial null-direction
   sphere bundle;
3. parallel/holonomy-preserved subbundle or tensor; or
4. characteristic, primary, or secondary bundle invariant

that carries the reciprocal representation and/or the Hopf structure without
choosing a coframe, carrier, action, topology, or desired particle result?

This is an object/type census. It is not a search for a Hopfion.

## Bounded scope

The audit covers:

- all object types already named in the frozen reciprocal-subbundle,
  null-section, coframe/Hopf, local-selector/holonomy, global-cocycle, global
  assembly, and complete-realization records;
- natural local constructions from the metric, orientation/time orientation
  when separately disclosed, `phi`, its first and second derivatives, and
  curvature through the registered two-jet class;
- global object classes supplied by a completed metric: Levi-Civita holonomy,
  parallel reductions, tangent/celestial-bundle characteristic classes,
  finite-cell cap/seam data, and conditional toric principal-circle data;
- nonlocal selector types already suggested by the complete metric
  (spectral, boundary, geodesic/causal, and variational selection), at the
  type/dependency level; and
- the complete 6,144-row registered local metric ensemble and twelve-family
  registered global completion taxonomy through their frozen evidence.

It does not exhaust arbitrary future higher-jet formulas, arbitrary nonlocal
functionals, unregistered four-manifolds, or future UDT axioms. It will not
turn that boundedness into a universal arbitrary-metric no-go.

## Candidate strata

Every candidate will be evaluated separately on:

1. conformal metric only;
2. metric plus orientation;
3. metric plus time orientation;
4. metric plus signed local `phi` and its derivative strata;
5. metric plus the registered finite-cell seal data;
6. each supplied completed metric/global topology; and
7. the combined currently registered UDT foundation.

Objects available only on a nonzero, nonnull, algebraically special, or
nondegenerate stratum will be labeled `LOCAL_STRATUM_ONLY`, never promoted to
a universal section.

## Independent axes

No one column may stand in for another. The census records:

- `intrinsic_under_local_frame_change`;
- `CSN_behavior`;
- `definition_domain`;
- `global_completion_dependency`;
- `object_type`;
- `reciprocal_content`;
- `Hopf_or_bundle_content`;
- `foundation_selection_status`; and
- `maximum_ruling`.

In particular:

- a bundle is not a section;
- a section is not a framing;
- a connection is not a topology;
- an intrinsic invariant of a supplied completion is not a UDT selector of
  that completion;
- an `S2` fiber is not a map to `S2`;
- a primary characteristic class is not automatically a Hopf secondary
  invariant; and
- a chart-level reciprocal character is not automatically a physical
  tangent-bundle reduction.

## Positive certification contract

A newly positive **native reciprocal/Hopf object** may be reported only if it:

1. is functorially determined by the metric plus already registered inputs;
2. survives arbitrary allowed local coframe/Lorentz changes;
3. has the correct declared CSN behavior;
4. is defined on the entire claimed finite-cell/configuration class,
   including admitted symmetric, flat, critical-`phi`, and seal strata;
5. requires no unregistered frame, plane, phase, section, circle action,
   periods, caps, orientation, boundary functional, carrier, or action;
6. contains an explicit, type-correct reciprocal representation;
7. carries an intrinsic Hopf datum—such as a selected map/section with a
   well-defined secondary invariant or a selected principal-circle bundle
   class—rather than merely sharing an `S2` fiber; and
8. is selected by current UDT premises rather than merely definable after a
   global completion is supplied.

Failure of any gate forces a scoped conditional, stratum, unordered,
unselected, or open ruling.

## Exact controls

The production derivation will independently compute:

1. the commutant and invariant-vector/two-form spaces of the connected
   Lorentz algebra on the tangent representation;
2. the commutant of its induced action on real two-forms;
3. the exact Lorentzian Hodge-star square and real eigenspace obstruction;
4. the no-fixed-ray consequence for the projective null sphere;
5. the admitted seal stabilizer rank census;
6. the domain failures of gradient-derived lines/sections at zero, null, and
   causal-type-changing strata;
7. the Frobenius property of a scalar-gradient one-form;
8. the registered 6,144-row curvature-algebra and simple-bivector evidence
   through frozen-source replay;
9. the distinction between open-path projector transport and closed-loop
   holonomy;
10. the dependency of conditional toric `c1`/Hopf data on periods, action,
    caps, orientation, and quotient; and
11. the type requirements for a Hopf secondary invariant.

An independent implementation must reconstruct the load-bearing exact
linear algebra without importing the production script.

## Preregistered falsifiers

The strongest negative wording fails if any current registered object:

- yields a proper frame-invariant reduction on every admitted stratum;
- yields a globally defined selected celestial section;
- provides a selected principal-circle bundle or selected map with an
  intrinsic Hopf invariant;
- supplies a holonomy reduction on the entire registered metric-active
  ensemble; or
- closes all required global data without an unregistered choice.

The strongest positive wording fails if an exact same-data frame
transformation changes the candidate, an admitted stratum makes it undefined
or ambiguous, a CSN transformation changes an alleged neutral object, or a
global/topological input is merely supplied rather than selected.

## Maximum allowed conclusion

The maximum result is a typed atlas identifying every surviving intrinsic
object in the bounded registered scope and stating exactly whether any of
them carries reciprocal/Hopf data.

If no object passes every positive gate, the maximum negative is:

`NO_FRAME_INDEPENDENT_RECIPROCAL_HOPF_REDUCTION_SECTION_OR_SELECTED_BUNDLE_INVARIANT_FOUND_IN_THE_BOUNDED_REGISTERED_COMPLETE_METRIC_SCOPE`

This wording may not be strengthened to an arbitrary-metric, arbitrary
higher-jet, arbitrary nonlocal, or future-UDT impossibility theorem.

## No-go boundaries

No action, field equation, carrier, source, boundary functional, topology,
orientation, physical scale, mass, time-live law, or GPU work will be
introduced. `LIVE.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `INDEX.md`, `MEMORY.md`, `CANON.md`,
fixed historical records, current registries, and research artifacts remain
unchanged.

# Complete-metric intrinsic reciprocal/Hopf object audit

Date: 2026-07-23
Mode: preregistered, metric-led, CPU exact algebra and frozen-evidence replay

## Result first

The audit finds one new exact, frame-independent, **real** reciprocal-shaped
reduction, but only on a disclosed local stratum of the complete registered
`(g,phi)` data.

Let

```text
alpha = dphi,
v = alpha sharp,
s = g inverse(alpha,alpha).
```

Where `alpha` is nonzero and `s` is nonzero, define the metric projector

```text
P = v tensor alpha / s.
```

For a two-form `F`, define

```text
Pi_parallel(F)(X,Y) = F(PX,Y) + F(X,PY),
Pi_transverse = I - Pi_parallel.
```

Because `P` has rank one, `Pi_parallel` and `Pi_transverse` are complementary
real rank-three projectors on `Lambda2`. They separate two-forms with one leg
along the `phi` direction from two-forms entirely transverse to it. Set

```text
J_phi = Pi_parallel - Pi_transverse,
D_phi = exp(phi) Pi_parallel + exp(-phi) Pi_transverse.
```

Then exactly

```text
J_phi squared = I,
star Pi_parallel star inverse = Pi_transverse,
star D_phi star inverse = D_phi inverse.
```

The construction is tensorial, independent of coframe labels, and invariant
under positive common-scale rescaling. Exact timelike and spacelike controls
both pass.

Maximum conclusion:

`EXACT_FRAME_INDEPENDENT_FIELD_ASSISTED_REAL_RECIPROCAL_3PLUS3_TWO_FORM_REDUCTION_IDENTIFIED_ON_NONNULL_DPHI_STRATA__HODGE_EXCHANGES_THE_SECTORS__GLOBAL_EXTENSION_PHYSICAL_OWNERSHIP_AND_HOPF_SECTION_REMAIN_OPEN`

## What is genuinely new

Earlier work established:

- the abstract reciprocal character;
- no universal physical reciprocal tangent two-plane;
- a conditional celestial null-direction `S2` bundle;
- no selected celestial section;
- an exact conditional reciprocal-toric/Hopf crosswalk; and
- no selected global completion.

Those results left open whether the complete metric carried the reciprocal
pair in a different representation. The present construction answers that
question positively on nonnull-`dphi` strata: the natural real carrier is not
a pair of named tangent axes, but a Hodge-exchanged pair of rank-three
two-form sectors.

This is a representation-level result. The projectors are derived from
`(g,dphi)` on their domain. Applying the already-derived reciprocal weights
to those sectors is an exact compatible realization. Current UDT does not
yet state that this is the physical owner of the founding reciprocal
character.

## Why metric-only Hodge structure was close but insufficient

For an oriented Lorentzian four-metric,

```text
star squared = -I
```

on real two-forms. The exact connected-Lorentz commutant on real `Lambda2` is
two-dimensional and is spanned by `I` and `star`. Any real equivariant map is
therefore

```text
a I + b star,
```

with characteristic polynomial

```text
[((lambda-a)^2+b^2)]^3.
```

It has no nontrivial pair of distinct real reciprocal eigenspaces.

After complexification, `i star` is an involution with two rank-three
eigenspaces, and

```text
exp(phi i star)
```

does give exact reciprocal weights. But unequal weights break the conjugacy
condition needed for a real two-form. The complex construction is intrinsic
and exact, but it does not descend to real geometry.

The nonnull `dphi` line supplies the missing real involution. This is why the
new construction is field-assisted rather than metric-only.

## Domain and global obstruction

The denominator `s` is load-bearing.

- If `dphi` is timelike or spacelike and nonzero, the real `3+3` split exists.
- If `dphi` is null, the unnormalized endomorphism
  `v tensor alpha` is nonzero and rank one but squares to zero. It is
  nilpotent, not a projector.
- If `dphi=0`, no direction or split is available.
- A continuous causal-type change must pass through a null or zero stratum,
  where the semisimple split degenerates.

The current foundation admits zero, spacelike, timelike, null, and
type-changing possibilities. In the frozen 6,144-row two-jet ensemble,
`dphi` is zero in 3,072 configurations, spacelike in 2,304, and timelike in
768; no null parent occurs in that bounded sample. Those counts characterize
the registered atlas, not solution frequencies or complete on-shell
universes.

A global bundle reduction would follow on any supplied complete branch where
`dphi` remains nonzero, nonnull, and compatible with the gluing. Current
Reciprocity, CSN, seal, finite-cell, and bootstrap statements do not prove
that global condition or select such a branch.

At the registered seal, `phi=0` does not imply `dphi=0`; the normal derivative
remains open. If the reduction reaches the seal, its two reciprocal weights
coincide there. Whether that occurs is a global field question, not a
consequence of the seal value alone.

## What survives without `dphi`

The complete metric still intrinsically supplies, under their exact premise
stamps:

- the conformal null cone;
- the conditional celestial `S2` bundle;
- oriented Lorentzian Hodge structure on two-forms;
- Levi-Civita connection and holonomy for each supplied representative; and
- primary characteristic data for each supplied global bundle.

These are genuine geometric objects. None by itself supplies the physical
reciprocal ownership, a selected section, or a Hopf secondary invariant.

The exact tangent-space controls reproduce the earlier obstruction:

- the connected Lorentz representation has no invariant nonzero vector;
- it has no invariant real two-form;
- its tangent commutant is scalar;
- spatial rotations have no fixed celestial direction; and
- the admitted seal stabilizer permits invariant projector ranks only
  `0,1,3,4`, not two.

The frozen curvature evidence also remains decisive within its scope:
5,376 metric-active configurations have a full irreducible curvature
algebra, while 768 flat configurations preserve every subspace and select
none. The registered curvature operators have zero isolated real simple
eigenbivector planes in all 6,144 rows.

## Hopf ruling

The new real `3+3` split is reciprocal-bearing but not yet Hopf-bearing.

On a timelike-`dphi` stratum, the transverse rank-three geometry has a
natural unit-direction `S2` fiber. This is another intrinsic sphere bundle,
not a selected `S2`-valued field. A Hopf secondary invariant requires at
least:

1. a selected section or map over a three-dimensional compactified domain;
2. transport/trivialization or an intrinsic bundle-level replacement;
3. physical boundary/framing data; and
4. a globally admissible completion.

None is supplied by the local split.

The prior reciprocal-toric principal-circle result remains exact
conditional: with periods, a circle action, primitive opposing caps,
orientation, quotient, and normalization supplied, it has `|c1|=1`. That is
the only audited object carrying an exact Hopf bundle class. Its global
inputs remain unselected, and no current rule identifies it with the new
`dphi` two-form reduction.

Primary characteristic classes of the tangent or celestial bundle also do
not fill the gap. They are invariants of a supplied global bundle, not a
selected `S3 -> S2` map or its secondary Hopf invariant.

## Complete object census

- frame descent;
- CSN behavior;

- Hopf content;
- foundation selection; and
- maximum ruling.

`DOMAIN_TRANSITION_LEDGER.tsv` records every `dphi` stratum.
`BUNDLE_DEPENDENCY_MATRIX.tsv` keeps bundle, section, connection, completion,
and Hopf-class dependencies distinct.

The census does not exhaust arbitrary future higher-jet or nonlocal
functionals. It is complete for the registered object types through two jets
and the typed global holonomy, characteristic, spectral, boundary, and
bootstrap classes named in the preregistration.

## Meaning for the broader program

This result changes the representation map without changing any particle,
action, or mass verdict.

The reciprocal structure need not be soldered to one named clock/ruler
tangent plane. The full `(g,phi)` geometry already has a natural
frame-independent place where a real reciprocal pair can live: dual
three-dimensional sectors of the two-form bundle, wherever `dphi` is
nonnull.

That observation does **not** establish physical ownership, global
persistence, a carrier, an action, or matter emergence. It does identify a
more faithful next question than choosing a coframe axis:

> Do the registered complete finite-cell equations or admissibility
> conditions force a globally nondegenerate `dphi` reduction, and if so does
> its timelike branch supply an intrinsic section or quotient compatible
> with the conditional toric Hopf bundle?

That is a future bounded audit, not launched here.
